Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion; si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	For when you treat it together, if the tip of the penis is not secure and is pierced, blackness and corruption come to the penis and testicles; so everything that is black and corrupt must be cut away, then apply a plaster made of honey and flour from pomegranate rinds and walnuts, then treat it with other treatments until it heals.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if there is bleeding, administer the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble: c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption; et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi; et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars; et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil; puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	The cauteries are of two types: for bleeding and for corruption; and if the tip of the penis is腐and retracted, one should insert a tube into the penis and let the patient urinate through it; and when there is hair at the tip of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, due to injury or abscess, then one should cut it with an instrument called a 剃刀, so that the foreskin is loose and the tip of the penis is free from all sides; and if it is a painful thing to discuss, one should cut it with a spatulum made of some soft wood at the head of the penis and the skin; then draw it gently apart and place a thin, moistened linen cloth in cold water between them so that it does not become erect again.
de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not a dislocation like other wounds; nonetheless, when we do this work of our own volition, and properly on infants, it is necessary that we make the best work, and the least harmful to health.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not teach the circumcision of their children, because they didn't use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experimentation.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	For I have seen the greatest part of masters and surgeons who performed circumcision all around, and in many places, and on all new-born infants; thus it happens that the foreskin shrinks because there are two membranes, and sometimes one membrane is cut above and the other below remains.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Then they recover consciousness, and the pain is doubled, and in the cleansing which is from the head there is not sufficient confidence in the movement of the limb; and in the cleansing of the fingernail perhaps the iron escapes and ruins the work, and many times it happens that they do not need cleaning and I have seen this.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	I have found the goodness of the experiment in the cleansing that is done with strong thread all along the length of the wound, for the stitches cut just as well above as below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues; puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens; puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens; puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien; et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge; puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	When you press your hand, you cut evenly across it; but the string should be well tied around the skin; and the method of the first operation is such that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only tying the string around the rod, and then you make him push it in every way you can; then you hold him straight between your hands, and support his weight with your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see any of the instruments; then put your hand to the rod and breathe on the wound, and pull it up until the head of the rod is in; then cleanse it well of the dirt that has gathered there, then tie the spot marked with a double string, then tie it under the other end; and hold it by the second ligature with your left hand, and pinch between the two ligatures, then quickly lift the wound and pull the head of the rod; then let the blood flow little by little, for that is the pus; and put powder on top of the powder, a cloth glued with an egg cooked in rose water, confited with good and fresh rosemary oil, and leave it until the next day, and treat it again until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The shape of the force for the purification is such that the two ears should be thin and pointed, and the ears should be as big as the palm equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	the error of the purification is when the incision within the ear drum; therefore, you must stretch it with your fingernail, so that the eardrum forms an abscess; and then, equally, cut it, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, hold it with tweezers, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent .iij. jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement; si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	And if it persists for 3 days, and what is under the eardrum is swollen, let it be until the abscesses are soothed and the skin slightly peeled; then cut it as much as you can, and beware of the part of the eardrum, it will not harm him at all.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point; cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore treat the site of a sudden wound with powder, as we said in the treatise on powders, and if it bleeds profusely and goes above, it will not harm; therefore treat it, as we said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	from retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division; et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e; et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	The retention of urine is due to a stone, or frozen blood, or a tumor, or similar things that we have mentioned in the previous section. If the urine is not released and you see that it is retained because of a stone which is lodged at the neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent over his knees, with his feet placed on his back, and his abdomen pressed down from above the back. The patient should strain as hard as he can, which forces the neck of the bladder to push out the stone, causing the urine to flow. If this does not work as described, and the patient feels great pain, then you must use an instrument called a "syringe." It should be made of fine silver, as light as the feather of a bird; its shaft should be one-and-a-half palms long, and slender at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede; puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine; et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And the way of the emission of urine is that you take a double thread, and tie to the end a little wool or cotton, and insert the end of the thread into the syringe; and soak up the excess wool and insert it into the syringe up to the root of the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and egg white; and let the patient sit on a seat, and lubricate the bladder and urethra with moist oil and olive oil and warm water; then gently insert the syringe into the urethra until it reaches the root of the urethra, then double the penis upwards towards the abdomen; then fill the syringe up to the bladder, and feel the patient's bladder emptying, and if this is not done according to this order, then the guide where it goes is wrong; then pull out the thread all the way through the wool, and the urine follows the wool, then pull it out, and let the urine flow; and repeat the syringe until the bladder is emptied and the patient relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	of bladder diseases
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scorching or bleeding occurs in the bladder, or pus has gathered there, and you see fluids and medicines seeping out, then use the entire instrument called "clepsydra", and this is its shape:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus: II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est; et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira; et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	It is closed and has three openings: two on one side and one on the other, as you can see. The location where the medicine is applied should be such that it blocks the urethra without any addition, so that moisture can be extracted and pushed in when needed. When you see your medicines seeping into the bladder, place the tip of the syringe into the moisture and suck out what comes through; this will draw the moisture back into the syringe. Then push the syringe strongly back in and release the moisture inside; it will now enter the bladder and the patient will feel it. This is the way of performing a subtle enema to cleanse the bladder.
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie; et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And it is made of silver or bronze and the head is higher; below, there is one testicle or two, then take a sheep's bladder and put in the moisture that you want to use to cleanse the bladder. Then tie it between the two testicles with a double thread, and heat up the moisture on the fire. Then insert the tip of the enema into the urethra and squeeze your hand on the bladder gently until the moisture enters; the patient will feel when the moisture reaches the bladder. If you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and cut it in a circle, and pierce small holes around it. Then thread a strong string through these holes, assemble the circle as you would assemble a shield, and put inside what you want of oil and moisture and water. Then do as you did with the bladder: squeeze your hand until the moisture enters the bladder.
de la piere	of stones
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already discussed in the division the methods of stone extraction along with medicines; and I have described the difference between a stone lodged in the ureter, and all the signs, and in which kind of stone one should operate; and in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will tell you plainly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that the stone which is lodged in the bladder happens more often to children, and it is a sign that the water passes from the bladder like water in its subtlety; and they open their arses, and the patient feels great pain in his penis, and they urinate many times, and then it becomes constipated; and most of these have a hernia; and healing is easier for children until they are four years old, and it is much more difficult in the elderly, and it is in between for those who are between youth and old age; and the cure is easier for those who have larger stones than for those with smaller ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, first it is necessary to cleanse the patient with an enema to draw out all the feces which is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For sometimes it clogs when seeking the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche dedens; se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	Then take the patient by the feet and tilt him upside down so that the stone sinks to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it comes out from the upper part; then let him sit between your hands, which are equipped with an instrument, and his hands should be under his thighs so that the bladder is completely tilted downward; then probe and touch inside; if you feel the stone in the opening, then hurry to cut on the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	And if it does not come out with the touch, then moisten your index finger of the left hand with oil, if the patient is an adult, or your middle finger, if the patient is a young person; and insert it into their rectum, and probe for the stone, and when you feel it on your finger, push it up to the neck of the bladder; then press with your finger, and move it away from where you intend to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And instruct the assistant to press on the bladder with his hand, and instruct the patient to extend his testicles upwards with his right hand, and with his left hand pull back the skin underneath the testicles in the area where the incision is made; then insert the spatulum, which is shaped like a spoon.
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans; par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And they cut between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the navel; and it should be straight above the stone, and both hands should be pressed against the anus, and the incision should be made across the belly so that it is wide at the top and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large; sometimes they press so hard on the hand which is against the anus that it pops out without effort; and know that there are some stones with angles and edges: these are difficult to remove; and there are some which are below, similar to a grape, and round, whose passage is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole; et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	And for those which have angles and edges, make the incision larger; and if it does not pop out, you should grip it with pincers which are like a file at the tip, to pull out the stone so that it does not slip away; or you put underneath a thin instrument with a curved tip; and if you cannot capture it thus, then widen the opening and if the blood comes out, stop it with vitriol; and if there is more than one stone, first insert the largest into the neck of the bladder, then push up, then pull it out, and then the smaller ones after if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it must be cut, and a larger wound made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces; et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	For two things happen to the patient: either he dies or the urine comes out through a channel that the wound cannot heal; but in any case, strive to pull it out, or scrape it away with tweezers, until you have removed it bit by bit; and when you have finished your work, apply incense, aloe, and dragon's blood to the wound, and constrict it, and place a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rosewater and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess; then re-bind the patient's wound on his neck, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen the bandages, wash the area well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment, until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit; puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And if hot abscesses and corrosions of blood come into the wound and there is congestion in the bladder, and the urine is retained in such a way that it can only exit with the urine: therefore put your finger in the wound and draw out that blood, for if any remains, then it will corrupt the bladder and burst; then wash the wound with water and garlic and salt, and assist the patient in every way you know how until he is healed; and it is necessary that each time you treat him, you bind his two thighs together and assemble the medicines on the spot.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	And if the stone is small and lodged in the urethra, and it is fixed there, and the urine cannot pass; then the treatment of what I have said above, that you cut many times, is an excuse for not cutting during this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already experienced this myself.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take an iron spike according to this form, and let it be tipped with three angles:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone so that it cannot go back into the bladder; then push the drill into the penis gently until it reaches the stone; and turn the drill with your hand in the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone from another side; then urine will flow out at once, then press your hand on what is left of the stone that is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides; et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it is broken at once and comes out with the urine, the patient is healed; and if you cannot do this because of something that hinders, then tie a thread under the stone and another one above it, then push the penis against the stone between the two threads, then pull it out and untie the string, and clean the clotted blood from the wound; and treat it until it is healed.And if there are many stones, treat them all in this way, one after the other.
de la piere des femmes	of stones in women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It sometimes happens that a stone becomes lodged in women's urinary passages, and if it does, the cure is difficult and prohibited for three reasons: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; the second is that one cannot find a good woman who reveals herself to midwives, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere; et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And the third way is that by chance one cannot find a woman who is well skilled in this art of medicine; and the fourth way is that the stone in a woman is deeper than in a man, so it requires a deeper incision, and there is great fear involved. And if necessity arises, one should take a needle and pierce the bladder, and if one cannot pierce it, do not desire to look for a finer needle; and present a mirror to a wise woman who understands the nature of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to do what you instruct her regarding the inquiry into the stone. And be very careful to check if the woman is a virgin; then she should push her finger into the vagina and seek out the stone; and if she finds it, she should press it under her finger, and recommend that she push her finger into the vagina where the pain is, and press her left hand firmly on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite; puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	If you find it, you must move it from the bladder gradually until it reaches the root of the thigh; then press on the stone at the root of the thigh towards the middle of the groin, where the testicle is located and feels the stone in that area; do not move your finger above or below the stone, and make the incision small at first; then pour water into the wound, if you feel the stone cutting through the flesh so that the stone can come out, and know that there are many types of stones: small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and some with veins.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	So you will know what it looks like to understand the diagnosis.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre; et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood vessels are broken and it is bleeding, then apply ground vitriol and hold it in place for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your work until the stone is out, and have some tools that I told you about in the extraction of the stone to help you with your task; and if the blood vessels are cut, and it's due to an artery that has been incised, then apply the powder to the site and use bandages and binding, do not re-open the wound, leave the stone alone, or else the patient may die; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the swelling has gone down, then return to your task and extract the stone.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	RamiCe aquoUSe n'Is aUtRe choSe QUe aSSemBlEe dE mOiStoR ou blAnC syfAc, QUI eSt dEsOz lOu keUr deS coiOnS, QUe cOnTIenT l'uef; et eSt apeLeZ «Syfac», et aUnqUoe fOIs eSt prOpReMEnt en La ToIlE dE l'uef, SI C'on cUIdE QUe CE sOIt .i. auTre oef; ET CeU n'AvIEnT Se poc Non.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this ramice is due to weakness that comes to the intestines, and that matter is spread out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus; et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And sometimes it comes from percussion on the testicles, and this moisture has many colors: or it is yellowish, or red, or black, or watery white, and so on; and these are the signs of how to recognize this condition, for if it is in the white syphilis that we have mentioned, then the abscesses are small, as long as an egg, and do not open the testicles, because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef; et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if there is moisture in the scrotum itself, then the abscesses are small with part of an egg, and so they think it is another egg; and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white syphilis, then it feels good. Therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, test throughout the entire scrotum, from which the form is as mentioned earlier.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, then, what comes after the foreskin, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz; puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions; puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir; puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue; et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when we treat it with iron, the patient should be healed according to his strength and the fullness of his body; then he should lie on his back on something slightly raised, and have lots of coverings under him; then he should sit up on his left side, and instruct the assistant to sit on his right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs of the heart; then take the spatulum and cut the skin of the ribs in between them from top to bottom, and let the incision be completely straight as you cut the skin of the ribs up to the white cartilage, and scrape it gently according to his strength; then pierce the cartilage with a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then put in your fingers, and lift the cartilage upwards; and do not touch the heart, but only the cartilage; cut all around it carefully, otherwise the water will come back; and if the egg has jumped out of your work, then put it back in its place when you have finished the work on the cartilage; then join the two lips of the ribs with a single stitch, and then heal it as you would other wounds, until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the wound corrupted by another disease, then you should tie off the vessels that are suspended, fearing a flow of blood; then cut into the wound throughout its suspension, extract the wound, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset; et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	And if water is gathered in two parts together, know that they are two blisters; then grasp the other part as you did the first equally, then wipe away the blood and put soft lamb's wool in oil into the wound; and put other soft lamb's wool in wine and oil on top of the blisters, and place doubled linen over them, and bind it all with a ligature following this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier; et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers; si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take two pieces of linen and fill them with lamb's wool according to this form, and sew them together at the groin of the breeches, and one of the heads press onto the fundament up to the back, and the other at the buttock; and the other two heads on the two angles, and have all the ligature tied in a loop of the breeches; and sometimes this blister is treated with cautery instead of cutting with iron, and it is that you grasp the thin blade cultellaire, and grasp the skin of the blisters, and let it be heated as we have said so that the white pus containing water is revealed; then take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that syfac at its edges, and scorch it with this fine hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille; et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And the cup in every way you can, as long as you stretch everything out; and be careful that the fire does not touch the egg; and know that this work is safer; and move carefully to prevent blood flow, and changes in the incision of the wound; and if nothing makes you contrary, or abscesses or blood flow or anything else, then cure what makes you contrary, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit; pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer; puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee; et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this procedure due to its horribleness, then administer piercing as I have told you, and when you are certain by the signs that we have mentioned that the water is gone, then have the patient sit on a high seat; then pierce the abscess in the part below to the full width of the spatumile, and insert the piercing tool deep into the body; and let the holes be wide so that all the water flows out; then put cotton over the area and tie it, and leave it to drain the remaining water, then treat the wound until it is healed; and if the white membrane does not allow the water to flow out through the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a pen or the instrument used to treat the water in hydrops patients, of which the shape is described earlier; and enlarge the wound, and know that the water will return, and will be assembled again after six months or so, and when it is assembled as before, and thus the patient will pass his days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse; et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	Know that in the dissection of this artery there are several dispositions which cause fear, and therefore it seems better to leave it alone. But I will tell you about its operation and the appearance of an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I therefore say that many abscesses come about in the body, and especially in the testicles; and this happens for many reasons.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion; et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief; et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	This is known as a suppurating abscess from an acute disease, either from an old wound or from a blow; and the color of the abscess is according to the color of the body; and there is no pain, and it is a grievous abscess; and sometimes there are grey, fearful, and pierceable abscesses with a flowing color, and occasionally they come from a vein, or from inflammation of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois; et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	When it is from a vein, it is known by the hot disposition of the abscess, when you press it with your fingers; and one must not touch it.Si li apostemes se fust si conus par le color de l’artere, si ne covient mie que tu le touches, car il est en la maniere dou mort.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars; et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	He who is made from the swelling of a vein is known by his appearance and the touch of the fingers, and anyone can make an incision on this appearance and on other marks; and you should cut the skin of the testicles, then the sac will be on top, and the white pus will come out, and release the suspensory ligament from all parts of the sac.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope; et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	If the sac is already infected with these sores, then you must cut it and open it; and if there is pus in the blood vessels, or in what is inside them, then you must release all those veins and cut them cleanly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the egg is in the rear location, then you must grasp it all and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is finished, then apply the wound with wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it heals.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait; et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	This is an abscess wrapped in a wrapper similar to a bud, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient suffers greatly when he walks; and the treatment of this disease is just as feared as the one before it, and yet we will tell you about its cure according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment; puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples; puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief; puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues; puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions; car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz; si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	It is necessary for you to make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then tie the suspenders of the scrotum tightly with your hands, as well as all the vessels that are close to the penis, and squeeze them firmly; then cut through the vessels with a sharp spatulum, exposing them, and then scorch from each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries in the temples; then insert a needle with a double thread where the vein first appeared, and tie it directly to the other end; then draw them together evenly according to the length of the body, and lead out the corrupted moistures; then cure the wound as in the others, or use bowels, so that any vessel that is torn does not nourish one of the testicles; for there is no harm in this, and if a vein appears in all the vessels, then draw the testicles to all the vessels so that the ureter does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rot of the eye socket
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions; et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses; et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement; et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	The causes of this hernia are through the incision that comes from the scrotum, or the extension over the abdomen in the region of the groin, causing the intestines to descend from that opening to one of the testicles; and this opening is either in the scrotum or from the extension of it, and these two types of hernias come from many causes: from a blow, or a jump, or a fall, or from lifting a heavy load, and from similar things; and the sign that it is from an extension of the scrotum is that it occurs little by little over a long time, and does not come suddenly; and the hernias are even all the way to the bottom, because the scrotum presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the sign is when it is from the section of the abscess, that it brings on sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses appear diverse, beneath the skin close to the surface, and that is for the exit of the intestines and the body from the abscess.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the intestines descend with the abscess, and are retained inside, and cause great pain to the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these cures of iron with fear, from which one should keep away.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir; puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes; puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc; puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir; puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars; puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille; et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement; et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz; puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz; puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars; puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne; et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi; et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant; puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	And the way to treat it is to instruct the patient to draw the intestines back into the wound with his hand if he can; then hold his neck between your hands and lift his hips; then press the abdomen above, and pull up all the skin of the scrotum from the bottom; then push in the edges of the incision with your fingers according to what you need to open the wound, so that the testicles can come out; then scrape off the scrotum that is under the skin of the testicles, until the hard white scrotum is exposed all around; then put your index finger into the opening next to the testicle, in between the white scrotum and the second testicle, and between the testicle and the second scrotum; and then move your right hand into the scrotum, and lift up the white scrotum towards your left hand, and lift the testicle up towards the scrotum; and tell the assistant to push the testicle up, and untie what is behind the ligature; and feel with your fingers if there is any of the intestine wrapped around the hard white scrotum, and if you find anything, then put it back into the abdomen below; then take a needle that has a thick thread made from ten fibers, and push it through the back part of the scrotum, which is after the skin of the testicles; then pull up the threads that appear, until there are four threads; then tie them together in the form of a cross, and tie the scrotum with a strong ligature in two places; then wrap the threads around the scrotum, and tie it tightly in two places, so that none of the vessels that nourish it can get through, and no hernia will come; then put the ligature back according to the first long ligature two fingers from that one; and after those two ligatures, leave the scrotum that is under the skin of the testicles hanging, as much as a finger's length; and then cut in the part that is under the skin of the scrotum, so that the blood flows, as we have said before; then apply soft lamb's wool soaked in oil to the wounds, and put on the ligature that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white cotton that we have described is cauterized after the incision, out of fear of bleeding.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece; puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	For this often happens, and leave the ligature in place until it cuts through; and if it is slow to fall out, then use hot water, and apply what we have said, until it cuts through; then treat the wound with another treatment, until it is completely healed.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz; puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the ancients say that it is made like the root of the weed, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after cutting above slightly towards the inside; then press gently, and treat the abscess with what we have described, until the vessels cut through; and treat it as we have said, until it is completely healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres; et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent; et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert; et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere: et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois; et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac; et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre; puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines; puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Sometimes the rupture occurs in the veins, as we have said, and the orifice opens; and no intestines emerge from the anus, and if some do emerge, it is a small amount, and one must keep watch over them at all times; and if they remain too long in this state, then the wound becomes putrid and suppurates, just as we have said, because the blood vessels are extended, then become soft and swollen and open; and it is treated with cautery, as we have already said; and sometimes it is treated with iron in the following manner: and the patient lies on his back between your hands, then press gently on the rupture where it is swollen with salt according to its size, about the amount of three fingers; then extract the blood vessel which is under the skin that has become suppurated, then take the vein and place it over the visible area of the blood vessel; and press it firmly into the abdomen, then cut the two visible ends of the blood vessel on the head of the vein, and cut them both; then extract the head of the vein, and do not cover or extend the suppuration or anything else, just as I have instructed you in the treatment of a rupture in the intestines; then treat it with the treatment for wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, clean and treat the wound until it heals.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The vein is constricted, and has no appearance in the rupture, and cauterization is more effective in this case, and closer to recovery.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the scrotum
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the scrotum softens in some men because the testicles within are softened, and it appears milky white; and when one wishes to treat it, he should make the patient lie on his back, and cut away the softened skin above the natural membrane; then join together the two edges with a single stitch, or up to four stitches firmly; then cut between the stitches, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	of chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	You should know that castration is considered evil in our religion, and for this reason I would prefer not to discuss it in this book. It is only necessary for two purposes: the first is so that the healer can answer questions about it and know how to perform the procedure; the second is because we often need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as bulls, rams, goats, and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	I say, therefore, that castration is performed in two ways: either by pullin
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	In the method we perform by pulling, we have the animal sit in hot water until the testicles become soft and pendulous; then we grip them with our hand until they come off and we no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Of the castration of a stallion: you should hold the horse still, and press the skin of its testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and strike each testicle once, after you have properly skinned them; and I leave some pus of the syphilis and the subtle syphilis which is over the vessels; and this manner of castration is better than that which is done by attraction, because with attraction something of the testicles might remain, causing the horse to desire lust; then cure the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	Hermaphroditism in horses occurs in two ways: one is that between the testicles there appears something like the form of a woman's nature, and it has hair, and sometimes urinates from it.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other way is in women, who have above the vagina a penis and testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	And the treatment of men and women is that you dress all the sores just as with other wounds; in the second way, men whose urine escapes through the skin of their scrotums have no cure.
de la tentigene	of the testicles
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	A tentwound is an open sore on the natural part, as long as it is too ugly to look at; and some women have them as large as a hand, and that is the cure for it.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	You must stain the excess of the tentwound with your hand or fingernail, and cover it lightly; and do not go too deep, lest bleeding occur, then treat it with another cure until it is healed; and for another wound that arises at the mouth of the sores, and apply it, and perhaps it will come out, and is like a cow's udder, and so they call it the "cow disease.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you must treat it, as we have said about the tendon, and cure it until it is healed.
de erratique	of erratics
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	It is erratique when the nature of the woman is not understood, or the passage is small; and it is natural from birth, or accidental due to illness that comes about; or it is caused by a foreign object, or from a subtle or thick phlegm, and it is formed deep in the womb, or on the sides, or below, or wherever; and they must be understood through examination of the vagina.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the tampon is nearby and apparent, grab it with your fingers or with a thread.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	If it is from a subtle phlegm and it is nearby the lips, do this: place your two index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread; then form the lips, so that the subtle phlegm is sucked in, and overcome the tampon; then take wool, moisten it in oil, and place it over the area, and have the woman rest at home every day, so that it does not adhere.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	If the syphilis is hard and thick, you must cut it with a spatulum like a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the wound is of fresh flesh, then dry it and cut it; and have blood-stopping remedies like açaí, dragon's blood, incense, and egg white; then insert a wide plug of wool so that the wound cannot close up; and let it be so for a long time, and then insert a tent of dry linen; then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when fresh flesh comes in the wound, it should be cut according to this manner, unless it is a deep abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For one must not touch an abscess that is deep in the wound.Et si il est alerge et pochon, si covient qu’il soit incisez sus li pochon et li alerge, si que il soit evacuez la mater, et que il ne vout remas.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins from which blood flows without a short-term remedy, and when hemorrhoids are old, they become throbbed; and we have already said in the section on their appearances, signs, and I will now mention those that can be cured.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and throbbed veins, when they are deeply embedded in the anus and do not appear upon examination, can only be cured by a cautery of fire.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the mouth of the anus, which one can feel, are those that can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	Therefore, you should place the woman in a cold room, then constrict the hemorrhoid with tweezers and pull out its roots, then apply a powder of restraining blood medications such as astringent acacia, dragon's blood, incense, and similar things; then bind her feet to the wall for an hour, then place her in cold water; and if bleeding occurs, have her sit in a decoction of sumac, pomegranate bark, gales, and similar things, then take barley flour, cook it with honey and garlic, and apply it as a poultice to her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it is stopped, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	If not, make him vomit with bellows on his back and breasts without piercing; then take woolen cloth, and moisten it in juice of plantain or in juice of dogwood with old wine, and apply it to the affected area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the abscess has drained, treat the wound with ointment until it is healed; and that which is called "albathir" is red and resembles rough skin, so it should be covered as I have said before; then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	and wounds of the anus
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscesses come about in the bowels, such as sores and piercing abscesses and herpes and hemorrhoids and hot abscesses, and many other diseases which I have mentioned in the section on diagnosis.Et quant li sang est vout de la veine ou de l’artere ou de la fime, si doit il estre curé a breff temps, si qu’il ne vienne al corps nule lesion.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	In this treatise, I shall discuss the hot abscess that appears in the body, which is not among the abscesses that form in the bowels; and if you wish to know how to treat it, observe whether the abscess is firm at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and whether it turns red when you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie; et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe; et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien; puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme; et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide; et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve; et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	Therefore, do not hurry to pierce it, but let the pain subside first; then have the patient sit on a chair, and have two small chairs for him to lean on, and support his back and rest his feet on something below his knees; tie his arms under his knees, and then suck the boil towards the right armpit, and insert the instrument used to open the abscess, after which its shape becomes apparent; when you insert this instrument, push it in only slightly at first to feel how deep the abscess is, so that what goes into the abscess does not go in further than it should, and does not hurt the patient; if the instrument is larger, cover the depth of the abscess with cloth so that it does not cause discomfort; then have him hold the cone-shaped part of the instrument against the abscess, and tighten the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit; et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec; et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites; puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez; et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites; puis reveigne a l’oignement.	And when the abscess is opened and they make it in the soft hand, then one must cover the head, or spathanum light; and when the bowels are emptied, then you should put in the wound tents moistened with rose oil, or with dry green oil; and put the tent out of the wound at the bottom of the injury, and put under the injury and over the small, clean lamb's wool moistened with water or mallows cooked; then heal after two days of ointment, until it is healed; and sometimes lift up the injury and the wound by enema of water and honey, and then with water or roots of iris and aristology cooked for a long time; then return to the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is drawn back into the injury, then you should be careful not to cook with iron, but heal it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir; adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui; et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost; car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification; et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	It is necessary for the midwife to first know the natural form of childbirth and its signs, which occur when you see the woman breathing quickly and desiring to smell aromatics. Then the child hastens to come out; then you know that this childbirth follows nature's course, and the afterbirth comes out with the child, and the mother is cleansed of her excesses through proper cleansing. But those who give birth in a different way do not give birth naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises; si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	Sometimes the child comes out feet first, or head first but upside down, or by the arms or the shoulder; sometimes it comes out from the stomach or the side, and it can get stuck in the neck or other unnatural positions. So the midwife must be wise and cunning in these matters, guarding against mistakes and disappointments, and I will now describe all the different ways to assist childbirth.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent; et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	If the baby is born head-first naturally but the mother is struggling and her vitality is weak, make her sit on a chair or have other women support her. Prepare an emollient of rose oil or fried fenugreek, and then the midwife should insert the small spatulum into the vagina to dilate it gently:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers; et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament; puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre: si istra maintenant l’enfes.	and split the amnion, and press his fingernail against it until the moisture within flows out; and press the woman's abdomen so that the child descends, and if it does not descend, then a clyster must be administered to the woman with a mixture of fenugreek and olive oil; then make her sneeze and cough from the condiment, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour: then the child will emerge.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc; et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut; puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement; et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.
